<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">On October&#160;27, 2022 we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.1. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter ended September&#160;30, 2022. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">The information furnished in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> under Item 2.02 and the attached exhibit shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01. Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">On October&#160;27, 2022 we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of November&#160;10, 2022, payable on December&#160;15, 2022. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be November&#160;9, 2022, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from November&#160;9, 2022, through November&#160;10, 2022, inclusive.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the First Quarter of Fiscal Year 2023 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">&#150;<I> Year-over-year revenue grows 5%, operating profit up 5%,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating profit up 4%</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at&nbsp;<U>http://investor.resmed.com</U> </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SAN DIEGO, October&nbsp;27, 2022 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced results for its quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>First Quarter 2023 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>All comparisons are to the prior year
period </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 5% to $950.3 million; up 9% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin expanded by 90 bps to 56.9%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross margin expanded by 40 bps to 57.6%
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Income from operations increased 5%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating profit up 4% </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Diluted earnings per share of $1.43;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted earnings per share of $1.51 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Our first quarter fiscal year 2023 results demonstrate strong sales growth in the Americas and solid overall performance for our businesses,&#148; said Mick
Farrell, ResMed&#146;s CEO. &#147;Our global ResMed team continues to power through the dynamic supply chain environment to increase production volumes and deliver more products and software solutions into the hands of people who need them. During
the quarter we saw strong customer uptake of our reengineered AirSense 10 Card-to-Cloud device. We also continued to increase our access to semiconductor communications chips, allowing us to produce more of our industry-leading, 100%-connectable
platforms. Looking ahead, we remain focused on delivering life-saving therapy solutions and driving accelerated adoption of digital health in sleep apnea, respiratory care, and out-of-hospital care. I am confident in our growth strategy and our
ability to accelerate toward our goal of improving 250&nbsp;million lives in 2025.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign
currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency&#148; basis, which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we translate the
current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to U.S. dollar
measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Discussion of First Quarter Results </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>All

devices as well as reduced competitive supply. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

factors discussed above and recovery of core sleep patient flow that was previously impacted by&nbsp;COVID-19. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

increased to 20.4&nbsp;percent of revenue in the quarter, compared with 19.5&nbsp;percent in the same period of the prior year. These changes in SG&amp;A expenses were mainly due to increases in employee-related expenses and increases in travel
expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$222.1 million, and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted earnings per share was $1.51, both consistent with the same period of the prior year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $44.7 million, reflecting the impact of increases in working capital. During the
quarter we paid $64.4 million in dividends. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Other Business and Operational Highlights </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Announced the acquisition of mementor, a German pioneer and health tech startup that develops and distributes digital
medical products in the field of sleep medicine and related areas. mementor offers the first permanently approved Digital Health Application (DiGA), somnio, eligible for reimbursement in the field of sleep medicine. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Celebrated the official opening of ResMed&#146;s new technology R&amp;D facility in Ireland (Sandyford in Dublin) and
announced a plan to double the Ireland-based software and technology team with 70 jobs over the next four years to support innovation, technology development, and product development. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Released updated global chronic obstructive pulmonary disease (COPD) prevalence numbers via a late-breaking abstract at the
European Respiratory Society Congress. Based on ResMed&#146;s updated research, it&#146;s estimated over 480&nbsp;million people worldwide suffer from COPD, a 22-126% increase over today&#146;s most cited resources. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The ResMed board of directors today declared a
quarterly cash dividend of $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of November&nbsp;10, 2022, payable on December&nbsp;15, 2022. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading on the New
York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Interests (&#147;CDIs&#148;) trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the
10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The&nbsp;ex-dividend&nbsp;date will be November&nbsp;9, 2022, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed
to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from November&nbsp;9, 2022, through November&nbsp;10, 2022, inclusive.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Webcast
details </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">ResMed will discuss its first-quarter fiscal year 2023 results on its webcast at 1:30 p.m. U.S. Pacific Time today. The live webcast of the call can
be accessed on ResMed&#146;s Investor Relations website at <U>investor.resmed.com</U>. Please go to this section of the website and click on the icon for the &#147;Q1 2023 Earnings Webcast&#148; to register and listen to the live webcast. A replay
of the earnings webcast will be accessible on the website and available approximately two hours after the live webcast. In addition, a telephone replay of the conference call will be available approximately two hours after the webcast by dialing
+1&nbsp;877-660-6853&nbsp;(U.S.) or +1&nbsp;201-612-7415&nbsp;(outside U.S.) and entering the passcode 13733726. The telephone replay will be available until November&nbsp;10, 2022. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">At ResMed
(NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier, higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for
people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our comprehensive&nbsp;out-of-hospital&nbsp;software platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their choice. By enabling
better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit&nbsp;<U>ResMed.com</U>&nbsp;and follow @ResMed. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Safe harbor statement </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Statements contained in this release that are
not historical facts are &#147;forward-looking&#148; statements as contemplated by the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. These forward-looking statements &#150; including statements regarding ResMed&#146;s projections of future
revenue or earnings, expenses, new product development, new product launches, new markets for its products, the integration of acquisitions, litigation, and tax outlook &#150; are subject to risks and uncertainties, which could cause actual results
to materially differ from those projected or implied in the forward-looking statements. Additional risks and uncertainties are discussed in ResMed&#146;s periodic reports on file with the U.S. Securities&nbsp;&amp; Exchange Commission. ResMed does
not undertake to update its forward-looking statements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">&#150; More &#150; </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, acquisition-related expenses and the reserve
for disputed tax positions from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">ResMed believes that&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted earnings per share is an additional measure of performance that investors can use to compare operating
results between reporting periods. ResMed uses&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;information internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating the results of operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information
provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides consistent financial reporting. The use of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of
net income and other GAAP measures. Like all&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;earnings are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under GAAP. </P>

current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to U.S. dollar
